        // Filter query
        var sQueryFiltered = $("#site-search-955107 input[name=q]").val().replace(/\?/g, '');
    $("#site-search-955107 input[name=q]").val( sQueryFiltered );

        if( $('#site-search-955107-term').val() ){
            return true;
        }else{
            return false;
        }
    });

                        var sBodyContainer = '.offcanvas-inner';
                        var sNavHeight = $(sNavContainer).height();
                        var iUnfixPoint = 0;
                        
                        if( __tnt.client.platform.ios ){
                            $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix-sticky');
                        } else {
                            $sNavScroll = false;
                            $(window).on('DOMMouseScroll mousewheel', function(e){
                                if( !$sNavScroll ){
                                    $sNavScroll = true;
                                    setTimeout(function(){
                                        var iFixPoint = $(sNavContainer).offset().top;
                                        var iCurrPoint = $(this).scrollTop();
                                        if( iCurrPoint >= iFixPoint && iCurrPoint > iUnfixPoint ){
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix') ){ 
                                                iUnfixPoint = iFixPoint;
                                                $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix').removeClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', sNavHeight+'px'); 
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix-top') ){ 
                                                $(sNavContainer).removeClass('affix').addClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', 0);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        
                                        $sNavScroll = false;
                                    }, 25);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
    </script>
    <div class="hidden-sm hidden-xs hidden-print" id="site-header-container">

                   <div class="card-headline">
                    <h2 class="tnt-headline">
                     <a class="tnt-asset-link" href="/news/local/govt-and-politics/realtors-say-zoning-can-help-market-create-more-affordable-housing/article_7c2740ee-8380-11eb-9aa6-8b49c7fb25d6.html">
                      Realtors say zoning can help market create more affordable housing
                     </a>
                    </h2>
                   </div>
                   <div class="card-meta">
                    <ul class="list-inline">
                     <li class="card-byline text-muted">
                      <span class="tnt-byline asset-byline" id="author-2569b38a-2a93-11e2-a3b2-0019bb30f31a-asset-7c2740ee-8380-11eb-9aa6-8b49c7fb25d6">

                      </span>
                     </li>
                    </ul>
                   </div>
                   <div class="card-lead">
                    <p class="tnt-summary">

                    </p>

                <div class="card-body">
                 <div class="card-labels">
                  <div class="card-label-section text-muted">
                   <a class="tnt-section-tag" href="/news/uva">
                    UVa
                   </a>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="card-headline">
                  <h3 class="tnt-headline">
                   <a class="tnt-asset-link" href="/news/uva/uva-law-clinic-assists-in-bill-allowing-inclusion-of-mental-health-evidence/article_98c52678-8824-11eb-aabc-d7d73a313a30.html">
                    UVa law clinic assists in bill allowing inclusion of mental health evidence
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                 </div>
                 <div class="card-meta">
                  <ul class="list-inline">
                   <li class="card-byline text-muted">
                    <span class="tnt-byline asset-byline" id="author-409fd64e-f003-11e7-a5ae-3b6be71044b5-asset-98c52678-8824-11eb-aabc-d7d73a313a30">
                     Tyler Hammel
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </div>
                 <div class="card-lead">
                  <p class="tnt-summary">
                   SB 1315 seeks to update Virginia law to allow people accused of a crime to present evidence of a mental illness, autism spectrum disorder, or intellectual or developmental disability to show they did not have the specific intent required for the offense charged.
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>

              <article class="tnt-asset-type-article clearfix card summary has-image image-right inherit letterbox-style-default tnt-section-business" id="card-summary-955114-328f8657-9b2c-59dd-ab68-2766454d53c2">

                 <div class="card-headline">
                  <h3 class="tnt-headline">
                   <a class="tnt-asset-link" href="/business/watch-now-is-the-shift-to-working-remotely-a-fad-or-here-to-stay/article_328f8657-9b2c-59dd-ab68-2766454d53c2.html">
                    Watch Now: Is the shift to working remotely a fad or here to stay?
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                 </div>
                 <div class="card-meta">
                  <ul class="list-inline">
                   <li class="card-byline text-muted">
                    <span class="tnt-byline asset-byline" id="author--asset-328f8657-9b2c-59dd-ab68-2766454d53c2">
                     GREGORY J. GILLIGAN AND JOHN REID BLACKWELL
Richmond Times-Dispatch
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </div>
                 <div class="card-lead">
                  <p class="tnt-summary">
                   "I dont believe we are observing the initial demise of the office like we believe we are with brick-and-mortar retail. But I do believe and I am convinced that is it going to be an evolved product in the foreseeable future."
                  </p>

  <script>
   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

        if (__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0) {
            __tnt.trackEventLater.forEach(function(obj) {
                __tnt.trackEvent(obj);
            });
        }

        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-track]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.track));
            });
